, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___peripheral__interrupt__number__definition_gga7e1129cd8a196f4284d41db3e82ad5c8aa6b8ff01b016a798c6e639728c179e4f}{FPU\+\_\+\+IRQn}} = 81

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
CMSIS STM32\+F401x\+Exx Device Peripheral Access Layer Header File. 

\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Author}
MCD Application Team 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxyVersion}{Version}
V2.\+1.\+0\+RC2 
\end{DoxyVersion}
\begin{DoxyDate}{Date}
14-\/May-\/2014 \begin{DoxyVerb}     This file contains:
      - Data structures and the address mapping for all peripherals
      - Peripheral's registers declarations and bits definition
      - Macros to access peripherals registers hardware
\end{DoxyVerb}
